add_namespace = sprd #dometstic
add_namespace = sprf #foreign
add_namespace = sprc #civil war

#Events affecting other countries are under 'Foreign Policy'

# Introduction event
country_event = {
	id = sprd.1
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.1"
	}
	title = sprd.1.t
	desc = sprd.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_alfonso_xiii

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.1.a
	}
	option = { #flavor
		name = sprd.1.b
		SPR = { country_event = { id = sprd.1163 days = 1 }}
	}
}

# Black Monday hits Spain
country_event = {
	id = sprd.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.2" }
	title = sprd.2.t
	desc = sprd.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NOR_black_monday

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	timeout_days = 14

	option = {
		name = sprd.2.a
		if = { #Only so debugging the scw at game start doesn't cuck you by adding black monday on top of everything else
			limit = {
				spanish_civil_war_will_happen_or_is_happening = no
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = released_after_annexation
				}
			}
			add_ideas = SPR_black_monday
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1181
					days = 3
				}
				set_country_flag = SPR_flag_black_monday_is_here
				complete_national_focus = SPR_Crossroads_of_Chaos
				set_stability = 0.25
			}
		}
	}
}

# Nerd Council Event
country_event = {
	id = sprd.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.3" }
	title = sprd.3.t
	desc = sprd.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	timeout_days = 14
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.3
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # mil focus
		name = sprd.3.a
		
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3a_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR_nerd_council_setup = yes
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_equipment_upgrade_xp_cost = -0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_war_support_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = -0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_experience_gain_army_factor = 0.1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # navy focus
		name = sprd.3.b
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3b_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR_nerd_council_setup = yes
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_equipment_upgrade_xp_cost = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_navy_org_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_experience_gain_navy_factor = 0.1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # air focus
		name = sprd.3.c
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3c_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR_nerd_council_setup = yes
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = -0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = -0.03 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_air_range_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_experience_gain_air_factor = 0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_air_superiority_efficiency = 0.1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # nuclear focus
		name = sprd.3.d
		add_political_power = -15
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3d_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_civilian_factory_use = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_sharing_per_country_bonus_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_scientist_xp_gain_factor = 0.05 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_nuclear_production_factor = 0.15 }
		}
	}
	option = { # general focus
		name = sprd.3.e
		add_political_power = -10
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = sprd_3e_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR_nerd_council_setup = yes
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_research_speed_factor = 0.025 }
			add_to_variable = { SPR_nerd_council_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.15 }
		}
	}
}

				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

# Alfonso Carlos Dies
country_event = {
	id = sprd.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.7" }
	title = sprd.7.t
	desc = sprd.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_alfonso_carlos

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SPR
		date > 1936.09.27
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = alfonso_carlos_dead
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = sprd.7.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		set_country_flag = alfonso_carlos_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.37
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}
}


country_event = {# Assassination of Luciano Malumbres
	id = sprd.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.9" }
	title = sprd.9.t
	desc = sprd.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPA_malumbres

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = sprd.9.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
				days = -7
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
				days = -7
			}
		}
	}
}

### Left Intro Events ###

# AP - CNT-FAI Talks Event
country_event = {
	id = sprd.13
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.13" }
	title = sprd.13.t
	desc = sprd.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_CNT_FAI

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	# Options for left intro #
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.a #Demand they drop syndicalism
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1188
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.b #Demand a more moderate stance
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.07
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach2
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:radical_socialist }
					has_coalition_with_target = yes
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:social_democrat }
					has_coalition_with_target = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1187
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1188
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.c #Continue the talks
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 24
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach3
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:social_democrat }
					has_coalition_with_target = yes
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1187
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1188
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.e #Walk out of the meeting
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_left_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = -0.07
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach4
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1189
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	# options for center intro #
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.f #Propose a ceasefire
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_center_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach5
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = sprd.1203
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.g #Demand they cut ties to france
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 39
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_center_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach6
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FRA = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = totalist
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1204
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1203
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.13.h #Propose a coalition
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_center_kingdom_intro
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		add_stability = 0.06
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.07
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_CNT_FAI_talks_approach7
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					power_balance_value  = {
						id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
						value < -0.3
					}
					NOT = {
						set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:paternal_autocrat }
						has_coalition_with_target = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1205
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.1204
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Arresting the CNT-FAI
country_event = {
	id = sprd.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.16" }
	title = sprd.16.t
	desc = sprd.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_zwolle_riots

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = FRA
						tag = ENG
						tag = SRI
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = sprf.5 days = 15 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sprd.16.a #Find the rat and establish a secret police!
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_idea = SPR_Tomas_Conde_de_Redezno_sec_pau }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister }
		add_ideas = SPR_Tomas_Conde_de_Redezno_sec_pau
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.16.b #We knew this would happen
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

# Street Violence in Malaga

			popularity = -0.03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
				days = 5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.18.b
		add_command_power = -25
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = 0.01
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final

	title = sprd.32.t
	desc = sprd.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = sprd.32.a
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { tag = SPR }
				FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = GER }
				}
				unlock_national_focus = SPR_join_germany
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = AUS }
				}
				unlock_national_focus = SPR_join_austria
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = ENT }
				}
				unlock_national_focus = SPR_join_entente
			}
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = { #France Support CNT Event Response
	id = sprf.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprf.2" }
	title = sprf.2.t
	desc = {
		text = sprf.2.d.french_accept
		trigger = { CNT = { has_country_flag = CNT_French_Support } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = sprf.2.d.french_reject
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SPR_CNT_No_French_Support }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_CNT_FAI
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprf.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			CNT = { has_country_flag = CNT_French_Support }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			CNT = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = CNT_French_Support_Granted_tt
				army_experience = 50
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 47590 }
					set_nationality = CNT
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 47591 }
					set_nationality = CNT
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = FRA
					modifier = KR_pleased
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprf.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_CNT_No_French_Support
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.07
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
}

# Carlists flee to Portugal

	title = sprf.3.t
	desc = sprf.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_javier

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprf.3.a #Allow them to continue operating from Portugal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = KR_hates_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = KR_hates_govt
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SPR
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprf.3.b #Break off diplomatic relations with Spain
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SPR
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprf.3.c #Wash our hands of the Carlists
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

	id = sprf.7
	title = sprf.7.t
	desc = sprf.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_por_salazar_franco1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event sprf.7 option sprf.7.a"
		name = sprf.7.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 112 } #Lisbon
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 instant_build = yes }
		}
		SPR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POR modifier = large_increase } }
		POR = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SPR modifier = large_increase } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Invitation into SOI Accepted
	id = sprf.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprf.10" }
	title = sprf.10.t
	desc = sprf.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIC_naples

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprf.10.a
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			ENG = { set_country_flag = BRG_in_faction }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Andorra
	id = sprf.16
	title = sprf.16.t
	desc = sprf.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_civwar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #end andorra
		name = sprf.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			1313 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_andorra_modifier }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_andorra_modifier }
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_andorra_modifier }
		}
	}
	option = { #restore it
		name = sprf.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		trigger = {
			1313 = {
				NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_andorra_modifier } }
			}
		}
		1313 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_andorra_modifier } }
		add_political_power = -10
	}
	option = { #keep it as is
		name = sprf.16.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sprc.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprc.3" }
	title = sprc.3.t
	desc = sprc.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_civwar3

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAR
		surrender_progress > 0.80
		NOT = { controls_state = 176 }
	}

	option = {
		name = sprc.3.a
		add_ideas = SPR_ready_to_surrender
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CNT }
			CNT = { country_event = sprc.6 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = SPR }
			SPR = { country_event = sprc.6 }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			clr_country_flag = sent_volunteers_CAR
			clr_country_flag = no_CAR_intervention
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sprc.121
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprc.121" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
		OR = {
			has_war_with = CAR
			has_war_with = CNT
			has_war_with = SPR
		}
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_of = {
					array = core_states
					var:v = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable_to_random = SPR_random
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { SPR_random > 0.92 }
				}
				country_event = sprc.122
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = sprc.121 days = 15 random_days = 20 }
	}
}

			}

				}

	}

		}

	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.402"}
	title = sprd.402.t
	desc = sprd.402.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.402.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_power_balance = {
					id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
				}
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
				value = 0.05
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
				days = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
				days = -10
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.556"}
	title = sprd.556.t
	desc = sprd.556.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPA_partido_sindicalista_7
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.556.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			prioritize = { 165 }
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
		}
	}
}

					character = SIC_Gaetano_Crocco
				}
			}
		}
		SPR = {
			annex_country = {
				target = SIC
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {

country_event = { #Morocco more like Poorocco
	id = sprd.1138
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.1138" }
	title = sprd.1138.t
	desc = sprd.1138.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SPR
		owns_state = 461
		owns_state = 462
	}

	option = { #release morocco as a protecterate
		name = sprd.1138.a
		release_puppet = MOR
		MOR = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = MOR_SPR_PUPPET
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = MOR_regulares_long
				name = MOR_regulares
			}			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mohamed Meziane"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/SPR/Portrait_SPR_Mohamed_Meziane_Spain.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_morocco_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_morocco_modifier }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_sahara_modifier }
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_sahara_modifier }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = SPR
				}
				remove_claim_by = SPR
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SPR_morocco_war
				}
				remove_ideas = SPR_morocco_war
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { #Intergrate Morocco (great idea!)
		name = sprd.1138.b
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MOR
				NOT = {
					state = 699
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_morocco_modifier }
				}
			}
			add_core_of = SPR
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SPR_morocco_modifier }
		}
	}
}

			factor = 1
		}

			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_1 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var = 2 }
			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_2 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var = 3 }
			}
			SPR_opposing_side_effect_3 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { SPR_opposing_side_progress_var > 3 }
			}

		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -50
		}
	}

country_event = { #Germany helps
	id = sprd.1201
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.1201" }
	title = {
		text = sprd.1201.t.germany_doesnt_help
		trigger = { SPR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_GER_agreed_to_help } } }
	}
	title = {
		text = sprd.1201.t.germany_helps
		trigger = { SPR = { has_country_flag = SPR_GER_agreed_to_help } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = sprd.1201.d.germany_doesnt_help
		trigger = { SPR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_GER_agreed_to_help } } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = sprd.1201.d.germany_helps
		trigger = { SPR = { has_country_flag = SPR_GER_agreed_to_help } }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 14
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.1201.a
		trigger = {
			SPR = { has_country_flag = SPR_GER_agreed_to_help }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_political_power < -20
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_pp_gain = political_power@SPR }
			multiply_temp_variable = { temp_pp_gain = -1 }
			add_political_power = temp_pp_gain
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 40
		}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
			value = -0.08
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
				days = 21
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
				days = 21
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_pleased
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.1201.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { SPR = { has_country_flag = SPR_GER_agreed_to_help } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_displeased
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# Country agreed to join Intergralist Entente
	id = sprd.1300
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.1300"}
	title = sprd.1300.t
	desc = sprd.1300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = sprd.1300.a
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				ROOT = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = FROM
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			ENG = { set_country_flag = BRG_in_faction }
		}
	}
}

	title = sprd.3009.t 
	desc = sprd.3009.d 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.3009" }
	picture = GFX_report_event_SPR_AP
		
	option = {
		name = sprd.3009.a
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
			
	option = {
		name = sprd.3009.b
		set_country_flag = SPR_no_banana
		set_country_flag = SPR_bau_i_nolla
		set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_oligarchy_subtype
		add_ideas = SPR_Joaquim_Bau_hog_pau
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.3009.c
		set_country_flag = SPR_no_banana
		set_country_flag = SPR_calvo_sotelo
		set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_maurrassism_subtype
		add_ideas = SPR_Jose_Calvo_Sotelo_hog_npo
	}
	option = {
		name = sprd.3009.E
		set_country_flag = SPR_no_banana
		set_country_flag = SPR_maetzu
		set_country_leader_ideology = pataut_hispanism_subtype
		add_ideas = SPR_Ramiro_de_Maeztu_hog_npo
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = sprd.4000
	title = sprd.4000.t 
	desc = sprd.4000.d 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sprd.4000" }
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.4000.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event option sprd.4000.a"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				add = 67
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 30
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment
			amount = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_power_balance = {
					id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
				}
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
				value = -0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
				days = 21
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
				days = 21
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SPR = { is_ai = yes } 
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.4000
					days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
			
	option = {
		name = sprd.4000.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event option sprd.4000.b"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_power_balance = {
					id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					add_power_balance_value = {
						id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
						value = -0.02
					}
				}
				50 = {
					add_power_balance_value = {
						id = SPR_burning_house_of_cards
						value = 0.02
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
						days = 14
					}
				}
				50 = {
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission_final
						days = -14
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
						days = 14
					}
				}
				50 = {
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = SPR_bop_opposing_side_does_something_mission
						days = -14
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SPR = { is_ai = yes } 
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.4000
					days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = sprd.4000.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event option sprd.4000.c"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SPR_SCW_ai_avoid_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SPR = { is_ai = yes } 
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = sprd.4000
					days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
